197extern void
198INT_CMrun_network(CManager cm)
199{
200 if (!cm->control_list->select_initialized) {
201 CM_init_select(cm->control_list, cm);
202 }
203 if ((cm->control_list->server_thread != 0) &&
204 (cm->control_list->server_thread != thr_thread_self()pthread_self())) {
205 /* What? We're polling, but we're not the server thread? */
206 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Warning: CMrun_network() called when another thread may already be handling the network\n");
207 fprintf(stderrstderr, " This situation may result in unexpected I/O blocking.\n");
208 fprintf(stderrstderr, " Server thread set to %lx.\n", (long) thr_thread_self()pthread_self());
209 }
210 cm->control_list->server_thread = thr_thread_self()pthread_self();
211 cm->control_list->has_thread = 1;
212 CManager_unlock(cm)IntCManager_unlock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 212);
213 CMpoll_forever(cm);
214}

222static thr_thread_tpthread_t
223thr_fork(func, arg)
224void*(*func)(void*);
225void *arg;
226{
227 pthread_t new_thread = 0;
228 int err = pthread_create(&new_thread, NULL((void*)0), (void*(*)(void*))func, arg);
229 if (err != 0) {
230 return (thr_thread_tpthread_t) NULL((void*)0);
231 } else {
232 return (thr_thread_tpthread_t) new_thread;
233 }
234}

450static attr_list
451split_transport_attributes(attr_list list)
452{
453 char *chosen_transport = NULL((void*)0);
454 if (list) {
455 get_string_attr(list, CM_TRANSPORT, &chosen_transport);
456 }
457 if (chosen_transport && (strchr(chosen_transport, ':') != NULL((void*)0))) {
458 attr_list new_list = attr_copy_list(list);
459 atom_t atom;
460 char *old_transport, *params;
461 char *next_param;
462 get_string_attr(new_list, CM_TRANSPORT, &old_transport);
463 params = strchr(old_transport, ':');
464 *(params++) = 0;
465 set_string_attr(new_list, CM_TRANSPORT, strdup(old_transport));
466 while (params != NULL((void*)0)) {
467 char *equal, *end;
468 next_param = strchr(params, ',');
469 if (next_param) *(next_param++) = 0; /* kill comma */
470 if ((equal = strchr(params, '=')) != NULL((void*)0)) {
471 /* there's an equal sign */
472 *(equal++) = 0;
473 /* we'll deal with this later */
474 }
475 while (isspace(*params)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) ((*params))] & (unsigned short
int) _ISspace)) params++; /* skip white */
476 end = params + strlen(params) - 1;
477 while(end > params && isspace(*end)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) ((*end))] & (unsigned short int
) _ISspace)) end--;
478 // Write new null terminator
479 *(end+1) = 0;
480 atom = attr_atom_from_string(params);
481 if (equal == NULL((void*)0)) {
482 set_int_attr(new_list, atom, 1);
483 } else {
484 char *tail;
485 long value;
486 while (isspace(*equal)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) ((*equal))] & (unsigned short int
) _ISspace)) equal++; /* skip white */
487 end = equal + strlen(equal) - 1;
488 while(end > equal && isspace(*end)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) ((*end))] & (unsigned short int
) _ISspace)) end--;
489 // Write new null terminator
490 *(end+1) = 0;
491 value = strtol(equal, &tail, 10);
492 if (strlen(tail) == 0) {
493 /* valid integer! */
494 if ((value < INT_MAX2147483647) && (value > INT_MIN(-2147483647 -1))) {
495 set_int_attr(new_list, atom, (int)value);
496 } else {
497 set_long_attr(new_list, atom, value);
498 }
499 } else {
500 /* string... */
501 set_string_attr(new_list, atom, strdup(equal));
502 }
503 }
504 params = next_param;
505 }
506 free(old_transport); /* not free'd by replace */
507 free_attr_list(list);
508 list = new_list;
509 }
510 return list;
511}

564int
565INT_CMlisten_specific(CManager cm, attr_list listen_info)
566{
567 int success = 0;
568 if (!cm->initialized) CMinitialize(cm);
569 success = CMinternal_listen(cm, listen_info, /* try others*/ 1);
570 return (success != 0);
571}

573#ifdef CM_DEFAULT_TRANSPORT"sockets"
574static char *CMglobal_default_transport = CM_DEFAULT_TRANSPORT"sockets";
575#else
576static char *CMglobal_default_transport = NULL((void*)0);
577#endif
578
579static char *CMglobal_alternate_transports[] = {NULL((void*)0)};
580
581static void
582CMinitialize(CManager cm)
583{
584 char **transport_names = CMglobal_alternate_transports;
585 char *def = getenv("CMDefaultTransport");
586 if (def != NULL((void*)0)) CMglobal_default_transport = def;
587 if (CMglobal_default_transport) {
588 if (load_transport(cm, CMglobal_default_transport, 0) == 0) {
589 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Failed to initialize default transport. Exiting.\n");
590 exit(1);
591 }
592 }
593 while ((transport_names != NULL((void*)0)) && (transport_names[0] != NULL((void*)0))) {
594 load_transport(cm, transport_names[0], 1);
595 transport_names++;
596 }
597 cm->initialized++;
598}

600static int
601CMcontrol_list_poll(CMControlList cl)
602{
603 func_entry *poll_list = cl->polling_function_list;
604 while ((poll_list != NULL((void*)0)) && (poll_list->func != NULL((void*)0))){
605 int consistency_number = cl->cl_consistency_number;
606
607 CManager_unlock(poll_list->cm)IntCManager_unlock(poll_list->cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 607);
608 poll_list->func(poll_list->cm, poll_list->client_data);
609 CManager_lock(poll_list->cm)IntCManager_lock(poll_list->cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 609);
610 /* do function */
611 if (consistency_number != cl->cl_consistency_number) {
612 return 1;
613 }
614 poll_list++;
615 }
616 return 1;
617}
618
619static
620void
621CMControlList_add_poll(CMControlList cl, CManager cm, CMPollFunc func,
622 void *client_data)
623{
624 func_entry *poll_list;
625 int count = 0;
626 poll_list = cl->polling_function_list;
627 while ((poll_list != NULL((void*)0)) && (poll_list[count].func != NULL((void*)0))) {
628 count++;
629 }
630 /*
631 * We're going to navigate the poll list without locks. This is
632 * somewhat dangerous, but safe enough if we only have a couple of
633 * functions so we never realloc. If we ever hit the realloc() below,
634 * there's a chance of some bad data references. At this point, using
635 * that many poll functions seems unlikely, but later, maybe not...
636 */
637 if (poll_list != NULL((void*)0)) {
638 if (cl->pflist_size < count - 2) {
639 cl->pflist_size *= 2;
640 poll_list = INT_CMrealloc(poll_list, sizeof(func_entry) * (cl->pflist_size));
641 }
642 } else {
643 poll_list = INT_CMmalloc(sizeof(func_entry)*10);
644 cl->pflist_size = 10;
645 }
646 poll_list[count].cm = cm;
647 poll_list[count].func = func;
648 poll_list[count].client_data = client_data;
649 poll_list[count+1].func = NULL((void*)0);
650 cl->polling_function_list = poll_list;
651}
652
653extern
654void
655INT_CMadd_poll(CManager cm, CMPollFunc func, void *client_data)
656{
657 CMControlList_add_poll(cm->control_list, cm, func, client_data);
658}
659
660extern
661int
662CMcontrol_list_wait(CMControlList cl)
663{
664 /* associated CM should be locked */
665 if ((cl->server_thread != 0) &&
666 (cl->server_thread != thr_thread_self()pthread_self())) {
667 /* What? We're polling, but we're not the server thread? */
668 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Warning: Multiple threads calling CMnetwork_wait\n");
669 fprintf(stderrstderr, " This situation may result in unexpected I/O blocking.\n");
670 fprintf(stderrstderr, " Server thread set to %lx.\n", (long) thr_thread_self()pthread_self());
671 }
672 cl->server_thread = thr_thread_self()pthread_self();
673 if (cl->network_blocking_function.func != NULL((void*)0)) {
674 cl->network_blocking_function.func((void*)&CMstatic_trans_svcs,
675 cl->network_blocking_function.client_data);
676 }
677 CMcontrol_list_poll(cl);
678 return 1;
679}

685static void process_pending_queue(CManager cm, void *junk);

687extern
688CManager
689INT_CManager_create()
690{
691 CManager cm = (CManager) INT_CMmalloc(sizeof(CManager_s));
692 int atom_init = 0;
693
694 if (!atl_mutex_initialized) {
695 atl_mutex_initialized++;
696 thr_mutex_init(atl_mutex)pthread_mutex_init(&atl_mutex, ((void*)0));;
697 atl_install_mutex_funcs((atl_lock_func)pthread_mutex_lock, (atl_lock_func)pthread_mutex_unlock,
698 &atl_mutex);
699 }
700 if (cm == NULL((void*)0))
701 return NULL((void*)0);
702 memset(cm, 0, sizeof(CManager_s));
703
704 if (atom_init == 0) {
705 CM_TRANSPORT = attr_atom_from_string("CM_TRANSPORT");
706 CM_NETWORK_POSTFIX = attr_atom_from_string("CM_NETWORK_POSTFIX");
707 CM_CONN_BLOCKING = attr_atom_from_string("CM_CONN_BLOCKING");
708 CM_REBWM_RLEN = attr_atom_from_string("CM_REG_BW_RUN_LEN");
709 CM_REBWM_REPT = attr_atom_from_string("CM_REG_BW_REPEAT_CNT");
710 CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL");
711 CM_BW_MEASURE_TASK = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURE_TASK");
712 CM_BW_MEASURED_VALUE = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURED_VALUE");
713 CM_BW_MEASURED_COF = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURED_COF");
714 CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZE = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZE");
715 CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZEINC = attr_atom_from_string("CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZEINC");
716 CM_EVENT_SIZE = attr_atom_from_string("CM_EVENT_SIZE");
717 CM_INCOMING_CONNECTION = attr_atom_from_string("CM_INCOMING_CONNECTION");
718 CM_TRANSPORT_RELIABLE = attr_atom_from_string("CM_TRANSPORT_RELIABLE");
719 }
720
721 /* initialize data structs */
722 cm->transports = NULL((void*)0);
723 cm->initialized = 0;
724 cm->reference_count = 1;

772static void
773CManager_free(CManager cm)
774{
775 int i;
776 CMbuffer list = NULL((void*)0);
777
778 INT_CMfree(cm->transports);
779 cm->transports = NULL((void*)0);
780/* free_FFSContext(cm->FFScontext);*/
781 cm->FFScontext = NULL((void*)0);
782 INT_CMfree(cm->in_formats);
783
784 for (i=0 ; i < cm->reg_format_count; i++) {
785 INT_CMfree(cm->reg_formats[i]->format_name);
786 INT_CMfree(cm->reg_formats[i]);
787 }
788 INT_CMfree(cm->reg_formats);
789
790 /*
791 * Applications are expected to free the user contexts that
792 * they request. If they do this, there will be no user formats to
793 * free at this point. (Doing so might result in double freeing.)
794 */
795 INT_CMfree(cm->reg_user_formats);
796
797 INT_CMfree(cm->pbio_requests);
798
799 INT_CMfree(cm->connections);
800
801 thr_mutex_free(cm->exchange_lock)pthread_mutex_destroy(&cm->exchange_lock);;
802
803 thr_mutex_free(cm->context_lock)pthread_mutex_destroy(&cm->context_lock);;
804
805 if (cm->contact_lists != NULL((void*)0)) {
806 i = 0;
807 while(cm->contact_lists[i] != NULL((void*)0)) {
808 INT_CMfree_attr_list(cm, cm->contact_lists[i])CMint_free_attr_list(cm, cm->contact_lists[i], "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 808);
809 i++;
810 }
811 INT_CMfree(cm->contact_lists);
812 }
813 list = cm->cm_buffer_list;
814 i=0;
815 while (list != NULL((void*)0)) {
816 CMbuffer next = list->next;
817 CMtrace_out(cm, CMBufferVerbose, "Final buffer disposition buf %d, %p, size %ld, ref_count %d\n", i++, list, list->size, list->ref_count){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?
CMtrace_init(cm, CMBufferVerbose) : CMtrace_val[CMBufferVerbose
]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - "
, (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing
? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file
, "Final buffer disposition buf %d, %p, size %ld, ref_count %d\n"
, i++, list, list->size, list->ref_count) : 0);fflush(cm
->CMTrace_file);};
818 INT_CMfree(list->buffer);
819 INT_CMfree(list);
820 list = next;
821 }
822 cm->cm_buffer_list = NULL((void*)0);
823 if (cm->shutdown_functions) INT_CMfree(cm->shutdown_functions);
824 INT_CMfree(cm->avail);
825 INT_CMfree(cm);
826 }

897
898 extern void
899 internal_add_shutdown_task(CManager cm, CMPollFunc func, void *client_data, int task_type)
900 {
901 int func_count = 0;
902 if (!cm->control_list->select_initialized) {
903 CM_init_select(cm->control_list, cm);
904 }
905 if (cm->shutdown_functions == NULL((void*)0)) {
906 cm->shutdown_functions =
907 INT_CMmalloc(sizeof(cm->shutdown_functions[0]) * 2);
908 } else {
909 while (cm->shutdown_functions[func_count].func != NULL((void*)0)) {
910 func_count++;
911 }
912 cm->shutdown_functions =
913 INT_CMrealloc(cm->shutdown_functions,
914 sizeof(cm->shutdown_functions[0]) * (func_count +2));
915 }
916 cm->shutdown_functions[func_count].func = func;
917 cm->shutdown_functions[func_count].task_type = task_type;
918 cm->shutdown_functions[func_count].client_data = client_data;
919 func_count++;
920 cm->shutdown_functions[func_count].func = NULL((void*)0);
921 }
922
923 extern void
924 INT_CMadd_shutdown_task(CManager cm, CMPollFunc func, void *client_data, int task_type)
925 {
926 internal_add_shutdown_task(cm, func, client_data, task_type);
927 }
928
929 static void
930 add_conn_to_CM(CManager cm, CMConnection conn)
931 {
932 cm->connections =
933 INT_CMrealloc(cm->connections,
934 (cm->connection_count + 1) * sizeof(cm->connections[0]));
935 cm->connections[cm->connection_count] = conn;
936 INT_CMConnection_add_reference(conn);
937 cm->connection_count++;
938 }
939
940 static void
941 remove_conn_from_CM(CManager cm, CMConnection conn)
942 {
943 int i;
944 int found = 0;
945 for (i=0; i < cm->connection_count; i++) {
946 if (cm->connections[i] == conn) {
947 found++;
948 INT_CMConnection_dereference(conn);
949 } else if (found) {
950 /* copy down */
951 cm->connections[i-1] = cm->connections[i];
952 }
953 }
954 if (found == 0) {
955 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Internal error, remove_conn_from_CM. Not found\n");
956 } else {
957 cm->connection_count--;
958 cm->abort_read_ahead = 1;
959 }
960 }

971 new_list->network_blocking_function.func = NULL((void*)0);
972 new_list->network_polling_function.func = NULL((void*)0);
973 new_list->polling_function_list = NULL((void*)0);
974 new_list->cl_consistency_number = 1;
975 new_list->cl_reference_count = 1;
976 new_list->free_reference_count = 1;
977 thr_mutex_init(new_list->list_mutex)pthread_mutex_init(&new_list->list_mutex, ((void*)0));;
978 new_list->condition_list = NULL((void*)0);
979 new_list->next_condition_num = 1;
980 new_list->closed = 0;
981 new_list->locked = 0;
982 new_list->has_thread = 0;
983 new_list->cond_polling = 0;
984 return new_list;
985 }

.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(trans->cm->CMTrace_file, "CMConnection_create %lx \n"

1050 extern attr_list
1051 INT_CMConnection_get_attrs(CMConnection conn)
1052 {
1053 return conn->attrs;
1054 }
1055
1056 typedef struct {
1057 int size; /*stream length to probe bw. */
1058 int size_inc;/*size=size+size_inc if previous size is not adequate*/
1059 int successful_run; /*if we have at least 5 successful runs,
1060 size is set properly*/
1061 int failed_run;/*After parameters are set properly, if we have 3
1062 contineous runs failed, we need to set the size again
1063 for the changed network condition*/
1064 CMConnection conn;
1065 attr_list attrs;
1066 } *bw_measure_data;
1067
1068 static void
1069 do_bw_measure(CManager cm, void *client_data)
1070 {
1071 double bw;
1072 (void)cm;
1073 bw_measure_data data = (bw_measure_data) client_data;
1074 CManager_lock(cm)IntCManager_lock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1074);
1075 bw=INT_CMregressive_probe_bandwidth(data->conn, data->size, data->attrs);
1076 CManager_unlock(cm)IntCManager_unlock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1076);
1077
1078 /*Initialization phase*/
1079 if(bw<0 && data->successful_run<5){
1080 data->size+=data->size_inc;
1081 data->successful_run=0;
1082 }
1083 if(bw>=0 && data->successful_run<5) data->successful_run++; /*if measured correctly in several back-to-back measurements, increase data->successful_run up to 5. 5 indicates parameters are well tuned now*/
1084
1085 /*After initialization, if network condition changed, and previously tuned parameters come to not adequate:*/
1086 if(bw<0 && data->successful_run>=5 && data->failed_run<5)
1087 data->failed_run++;
1088 if(bw>=0) data->failed_run=0; /*guard for contineous failures. */
1089 if(data->failed_run>=5){ /*need to tune parameters again now. */
1090 data->successful_run=0;
1091 data->failed_run=0;
1092 }
1093
1094 CMtrace_out(data->conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose,"successful run: %d, failed run: %d, size: %d, bw: %f\n", data->successful_run, data->failed_run, data->size, bw){struct timespec ts ; (((data->conn->cm->CMTrace_file
== ((void*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(data->conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose
) : CMtrace_val[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(
data->conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid
(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime
(1, &ts),fprintf(data->conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(data->conn->
cm->CMTrace_file, "successful run: %d, failed run: %d, size: %d, bw: %f\n"
, data->successful_run, data->failed_run, data->size
, bw) : 0);fflush(data->conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
1095 return;
1096 }

1098 extern int
1099 INT_CMConnection_set_character(CMConnection conn, attr_list attrs)
1100 {
1101 long interval_value;
1102 if (attrs == NULL((void*)0)) return 0;
1103 if (get_long_attr(attrs, CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL, &interval_value)) {
1104 bw_measure_data data;
1105 int previous_interval;
1106 CMTaskHandle task = NULL((void*)0);
1107 if ((interval_value <= 1) || (interval_value > 60*60*8)) {
1108 printf("Bad CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL, %ld seconds\n",
1109 interval_value);
1110 return 0;
1111 }
1112
1113 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose,"CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL set, interval is %ld\n", interval_value){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL set, interval is %ld\n"
, interval_value) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
1114 if (conn->characteristics &&
1115 (get_int_attr(conn->characteristics, CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL,
1116 &previous_interval) != 0)) {
1117 CMTaskHandle prior_task = NULL((void*)0);
1118 if (interval_value >= previous_interval) {
1119 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose,"CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL prior interval is %d, no action.\n", previous_interval){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL prior interval is %d, no action.\n"
, previous_interval) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file
);};
1120 return 1;
1121 }
1122 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose,"CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL prior interval is %d, killing prior task.\n", previous_interval){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL prior interval is %d, killing prior task.\n"
, previous_interval) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file
);};
1123 get_long_attr(conn->characteristics, CM_BW_MEASURE_TASK,
1124 (long*)(long)&prior_task);
1125 if (prior_task) {
1126 INT_CMremove_task(prior_task);
1127 set_long_attr(conn->characteristics, CM_BW_MEASURE_TASK, (long)0);
1128 }
1129 }
1130 data = malloc(sizeof(*data));
1131 data->size=data->size_inc=-1;
1132
1133 /*Get attr about size, size_inc from attributes. */
1134 get_int_attr(attrs, CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZE, &(data->size));
1135 if(data->size<1024)
1136 data->size=1024;
1137 get_int_attr(attrs, CM_BW_MEASURE_SIZEINC, &(data->size_inc));
1138 if(data->size_inc<1024)
1139 data->size_inc=1024;
1140
1141 data->successful_run=0;
1142 data->failed_run=0;
1143
1144 /*app set attr about N and repeat time. store in data->attrs automically and pass to regressive_probe_bandwidth.
1145 */
1146 data->conn = conn;
1147 data->attrs = CMattr_copy_list(conn->cm, attrs)CMint_attr_copy_list(conn->cm, attrs, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1147);
1148 /* do one task almost immediately */
1149 task = INT_CMadd_delayed_task(conn->cm, 0, 1000, do_bw_measure,
1150 (void*)data);
1151 free(task);
1152 /* schedule tasks periodically */
1153 task = INT_CMadd_periodic_task(conn->cm, interval_value, 0,
1154 do_bw_measure, (void*)data);
1155 if (conn->characteristics == NULL((void*)0)) {
1156 conn->characteristics = CMcreate_attr_list(conn->cm)CMint_create_attr_list(conn->cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1156);
1157 }
1158 set_int_attr(conn->characteristics, CM_BW_MEASURE_INTERVAL,
1159 interval_value);
1160 set_long_attr(conn->characteristics, CM_BW_MEASURE_TASK, (long)task);
1161
1162 return 1;
1163 }
1164 return 0;
1165 }

1287 *lastp = entry;

1370 #define CURRENT_HANDSHAKE_VERSION1 1
1371
1372 static
1373 int
1374 transport_is_reliable(CMConnection conn)
1375 {
1376 attr_list list;
1377 int ret;
1378 if (conn->trans->get_transport_characteristics == NULL((void*)0)) {
1379 return 0; /* don't know */
1380 }
1381 list = conn->trans->get_transport_characteristics(conn->trans, &CMstatic_trans_svcs,
1382 conn->trans->trans_data);
1383 if (!get_int_attr(list, CM_TRANSPORT_RELIABLE, &ret)) {
1384 return 0; /* don't know */
1385 }
1386 return ret;
1387 }

1389 static
1390 void
1391 send_and_maybe_wait_for_handshake(CManager cm, CMConnection conn)
1392 {
1393 struct FFSEncodeVec tmp_vec[1];
1394 int reliable = transport_is_reliable(conn);
1395 int msg[5], actual;
1396 if (!cm->FFSserver_identifier) cm->FFSserver_identifier = -1;
1397 msg[0] = 0x434d4800; /* CMH\0 */
1398 msg[1] = (CURRENT_HANDSHAKE_VERSION1 << 24) + sizeof(msg);
1399 msg[2] = cm->FFSserver_identifier;
1400 msg[3] = 5; /* not implemented yet */
1401 msg[4] = 0; /* not implemented yet */
1402 if (conn->remote_format_server_ID != 0) {
1403 /* set high bit if we already have his ID */
1404 msg[3] |= 0x80000000;
1405 }
1406 tmp_vec[0].iov_base = &msg;
1407 tmp_vec[0].iov_len = sizeof(msg);
1408 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "CM - sending handshake\n"){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void

()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "CM - sending handshake\n"
) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
1409 if ((conn->remote_format_server_ID == 0) && reliable) {
1410 /* we will await his respone */
1411 conn->handshake_condition = INT_CMCondition_get(cm, conn);
1412 }
1413 actual = conn->trans->writev_func(&CMstatic_trans_svcs,
1414 conn->transport_data,
1415 &tmp_vec[0], 1, NULL((void*)0));
1416

, conn->write_pending) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file
);};

1512 {

1521 conn->buffer_full_point, conn->buffer_data_end);

1523 }

1617 int
1618 INT_CMcontact_self_check(CManager cm, attr_list attrs)
1619 {
1620 transport_entry *trans_list;
1621 if (!cm->initialized) CMinitialize(cm);
1622 trans_list = cm->transports;
1623 while ((trans_list != NULL((void*)0)) && (*trans_list != NULL((void*)0))) {
1624 int result = 0;
1625 result = (*trans_list)->self_check(cm, &CMstatic_trans_svcs,
1626 *trans_list, attrs);
1627 if (result) return result;
1628 trans_list++;
1629 }
1630 return 0;
1631 }

1750 extern CMbuffer
1751 cm_extend_data_buf(CManager cm, CMbuffer tmp, int length)
1752 {
1753 (void)cm;

1760 tmp->size = length;
1761 }
1762 return tmp;
1763 }

1771 if ((cmb->ref_count == 0) && (cmb->return_callback != NULL((void*)0))) {
1772 CMbuffer last = NULL((void*)0), tmp = cm->cm_buffer_list;
1773 /* UNLINK */
1774 CMtrace_out(cm, CMBufferVerbose, "cm_return_data_buf --- Unlinking %p cmb\n", cmb){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?

1775 while (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1776 if (tmp != cmb) {
1777 last = tmp;
1778 tmp = tmp->next;
1779 continue;
1780 }
1781 /* remove the buffer from CM's list */
1782 if (last == NULL((void*)0)) {
1783 cm->cm_buffer_list = tmp->next;
1784 } else {
1785 last->next = tmp->next;
1786 }
1787 tmp = tmp->next;
1788 (cmb->return_callback)(cmb->return_callback_data);
1789 free(cmb);
1790 break;
1791 }
1792 }
1793 }
1794
1795 static CMbuffer
1796 cm_buffer_lookup(CManager cm, void *buffer)
1797 {
1798 CMbuffer tmp = cm->cm_buffer_list;
1799 while (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1800 if ((tmp->buffer <= buffer) &&
1801 ((char*)buffer < ((char*)tmp->buffer + tmp->size))){
1802 return tmp;
1803 }
1804 tmp = tmp->next;
1805 }
1806 return NULL((void*)0);
1807 }
1808
1809 static CMbuffer
1810 cm_buffer_dump_list(CManager cm)
1811 {
1812 CMbuffer tmp = cm->cm_buffer_list;
1813 printf("Known CM buffers are:\n");
1814 while (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1815 printf("Buffer begin %p, size %ld, end %p\n",
1816 tmp->buffer, tmp->size, (char*)tmp->buffer + tmp->size);
1817 tmp = tmp->next;
1818 }
1819 return NULL((void*)0);
1820 }

1822 int (*cm_write_hook)(int) = (int (*)(int)) NULL((void*)0);

1824 void (*cm_postread_hook)(int,char*) = (void (*)(int, char*)) NULL((void*)0);
1825 void (*cm_last_postread_hook)() = (void (*)()) NULL((void*)0);

1827
1828 static void process_pending_queue(CManager cm, void *junk)
1829 {
1830 /* shortcircuit if no data, no lock */
1831 if (!cm->pending_data_queue) return;
1832
1833 CManager_lock(cm)IntCManager_lock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1833);
1834 while (cm->pending_data_queue) {
1835 pending_queue entry = cm->pending_data_queue;
1836 int result;
1837 cm->pending_data_queue = entry->next;
1838 result = CMact_on_data(entry->conn, entry->buffer, entry->buffer->buffer, entry->length);
1839 if (result != 0) {
1840 printf("in process pending, CMact_on_data returned %d\n", result);
1841 }
1842 cm_return_data_buf(cm, entry->buffer);
1843 free(entry);
1844 }
1845 CManager_unlock(cm)IntCManager_unlock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1845);
1846 }
1847
1848 static void add_buffer_to_pending_queue(CManager cm, CMConnection conn, CMbuffer buf, long length)
1849 {
1850 assert(CManager_locked(cm))((void) sizeof ((CManager_locked(cm)) ? 1 : 0), __extension__
({ if (CManager_locked(cm)) ; else __assert_fail ("CManager_locked(cm)"
, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c", 1850, __extension__
__PRETTY_FUNCTION__); }));
1851 pending_queue entry = malloc(sizeof(struct pending_queue_entry));
1852 entry->next = NULL((void*)0);
1853 entry->conn = conn;
1854 entry->buffer = buf;
1855 entry->length = length;
1856 if (!cm->pending_data_queue) {
1857 cm->pending_data_queue = entry;
1858 } else {
1859 pending_queue last = cm->pending_data_queue;
1860 pending_queue tmp = last->next;
1861 while (tmp) {
1862 last = tmp;
1863 tmp = tmp->next;
1864 }
1865 last->next = entry;
1866 }
1867 CMwake_server_thread(cm);
1868 }

1870 static
1871 CMbuffer
1872 fill_cmbuffer(CManager cm, char *buf, long length)
1873 {
1874 CMbuffer ret = cm_get_data_buf(cm, length);
1875 memcpy(ret->buffer, buf, length);
1876 return ret;
1877 }

1879 extern void CMDataAvailable(transport_entry trans, CMConnection conn)
1880 {
1881 CManager cm = conn->cm;
1882 int do_read = 1;
1883 int read_msg_count = 0;
1884 long read_byte_count = 0;
1885 int result;
1886 static int first = 1;
1887 static int read_ahead_msg_limit = 50;
1888 static long read_ahead_byte_limit = 1024*1024*1024;
1889 static int use_blocking_reads = 1;
1890 int first_four = 0;
1891 char *tmp_message_buffer = NULL((void*)0);
1892 int data_length;
1893 CMbuffer message_buffer;
1894 long buffer_full_point, buffer_data_end;
1895
1896 /* called from the transport, grab the locks */
1897 if (first) {
1898 char *tmp;
1899 first = 0;
1900 tmp = getenv("CMReadAheadMsgLimit");
1901 if (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1902 if (sscanf(tmp, "%d", &read_ahead_msg_limit) != 1) {
1903 printf("Read ahead msg limit \"%s\" not parsed\n", tmp);
1904 }
1905 }
1906 tmp = getenv("CMReadAheadByteLimit");
1907 if (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1908 if (sscanf(tmp, "%ld", &read_ahead_byte_limit) != 1) {
1909 printf("Read ahead byte limit \"%s\" not parsed\n", tmp);
1910 }
1911 }
1912 tmp = getenv("CMBlockingReads");
1913 if (tmp != NULL((void*)0)) {
1914 use_blocking_reads = atoi(tmp);
1915 }
1916 }
1917
1918 if (conn->buffer_full_point == 0) {
1919 /* nothing saved from last invocation */
1920 message_buffer = NULL((void*)0);
1921 buffer_full_point = 0;
1922 buffer_data_end = 0;
1923 } else {
1924 /* message_buffer, buffer_full_point and buffer_data_end cached from last call to CMDataAvailable */
1925 message_buffer = conn->message_buffer;
1926 conn->message_buffer = NULL((void*)0);
1927 buffer_full_point = conn->buffer_full_point;
1928 conn->buffer_full_point = 0;
1929 buffer_data_end = conn->buffer_data_end;
1930 conn->buffer_data_end = 0;
1931 }
1932 start_read:
1933 if (conn->failed) {
1934 return;
1935 }
1936 if (buffer_full_point == 0) {
1937 buffer_full_point = 4; /* read first 4 bytes first thing */
1938 buffer_data_end = 0; /* no bytes read yet */
1939 first_four = 1;
1940 }
1941 if (trans->read_to_buffer_func) {
1942 CMtrace_out(cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "CMdata continuing read, already have %ld bytes, trying to read total %ld\n", buffer_data_end, buffer_full_point){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?

]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - "
, (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing
? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file
, "CMdata continuing read, already have %ld bytes, trying to read total %ld\n"
, buffer_data_end, buffer_full_point) : 0);fflush(cm->CMTrace_file
);};
1943 } else {
1944 CMtrace_out(cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "CMdata block read beginning\n"){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?
CMtrace_init(cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val[CMLowLevelVerbose
]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - "
, (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing
? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file
, "CMdata block read beginning\n") : 0);fflush(cm->CMTrace_file
);};
1945 }
1946 if (buffer_full_point < HEADER_BUFFER_SIZE20) {
1947 tmp_message_buffer = &conn->header_buffer[0];
1948 } else {
1949 if (message_buffer == NULL((void*)0)) {
1950 /* we had data in the header buffer, but need more space */
1951 message_buffer = cm_get_data_buf(cm, buffer_full_point);
1952 memcpy(message_buffer->buffer, &conn->header_buffer[0],
1953 buffer_data_end);
1954 tmp_message_buffer = message_buffer->buffer;
1955 } else {
1956 /* make sure buffer is big enough */
1957 cm_extend_data_buf(cm, message_buffer, buffer_full_point);
1958 tmp_message_buffer = message_buffer->buffer;
1959 }
1960 }
1961 if (cm_preread_hook) {
1962 do_read = cm_preread_hook(buffer_full_point - buffer_data_end, tmp_message_buffer);
1963 }
1964 if (do_read) {
1965 if (trans->read_to_buffer_func) {
1966 /*
1967 * read_to_buffer functionality present means we can read the transport directly to any memory area
1968 * This gives us the most flexibility in managing our data.
1969 * At this point, tmp_message_buffer is the char* buffer to which we want to read
1970 * If non-NULL, message_buffer is the CMBuffer that holds this memory
1971 * buffer_data_end is how much data is already in the buffer
1972 * buffer_full_point is how much data we think we need for the message to be complete
1973 */
1974 int read_len = buffer_full_point - buffer_data_end;
1975 char *read_target_buf = tmp_message_buffer + buffer_data_end;
1976 /*
1977 * non blocking is True only if :
1978 * - we're reading the first four bytes (first_four is true) and use_read_thread is false
1979 * - or use_blocking_reads is false and use_read_thread is false
1980 */
1981 int non_blocking = first_four || !use_blocking_reads;
1982 int actual;
1983 if (conn->use_read_thread) {
1984 non_blocking = 0;
1985 CManager_unlock(cm)IntCManager_unlock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 1985);
1986 }
1987 if (read_len == 0) {
1988 /* should never happen that we are here but don't need more data */
1989 printf("Seriously bad shit\n");
1990 }

1992 conn->transport_data,
1993 read_target_buf, read_len, non_blocking);
1994 if (conn->use_read_thread) {
1995 CManager_lock(cm)IntCManager_lock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"

2088 static void
2089 CMdo_handshake(CMConnection conn, int handshake_version, int byte_swap, char *base)
2090 {
2091 int do_send = 1;
2092 int remote_format_server_ID;
2093 int remote_CManager_ID;
2094 if (byte_swap) {
2095 ((char*)&remote_format_server_ID)[0] = base[3];
2096 ((char*)&remote_format_server_ID)[1] = base[2];
2097 ((char*)&remote_format_server_ID)[2] = base[1];
2098 ((char*)&remote_format_server_ID)[3] = base[0];

2100 ((char*)&remote_CManager_ID)[1] = base[6];

) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2109 if ((remote_CManager_ID & 0x80000000) == 0x80000000) {
2110 /* the other fellow already has our ID */
2111 do_send = 0;
2112 remote_CManager_ID ^= 0x80000000; /* kill high bit */

2139 static int
2140 CMact_on_data(CMConnection conn, CMbuffer cm_buffer, char *buffer, long length)
2141 {

2143 char *check_sum_base = buffer;
2144 int byte_swap = 0;
2145 int get_attrs = 0;
2146 int skip = 0;
2147 int performance_msg = 0, event_msg = 0, evcontrol_msg = 0, handshake = 0;
2148 int performance_func = 0, handshake_version = 0;
2149 CMbuffer cm_decode_buf = NULL((void*)0);
2150 attr_list attrs = NULL((void*)0);
2151 int64_t data_length, decoded_length;
2152 int attr_length = 0, i;

2158 CMincoming_format_list cm_format = NULL((void*)0);
2159 int message_key;
2160 unsigned char checksum;
2161 int short_length = 1;
2162
2163 if (length < 4) {
2164 return 4 - length;
2165 }
2166 message_key = 0x00ffff00 & *((int*)buffer);
2167 switch (message_key) { /* assume 4-byte int */
2168 case 0x00444d00: /* \0DMC reversed byte order */
2169 byte_swap = 1;
2170 case 0x004d4400: /* CMD\0 */
2171 break;
2172 case 0x00414d00: /* \0AMC reversed byte order */
2173 byte_swap = 1;
2174 case 0x004d4100: /* CMA\0 */
2175 get_attrs = 1;
2176 break;
2177 case 0x00005645: /* \0CVE reversed byte order */
2178 byte_swap = 1;
2179 case 0x45560000: /* EVC\0 */
2180 evcontrol_msg = 1;
2181 break;
2182 case 0x00504d00: /* \0PMC reversed byte order */
2183 byte_swap = 1;
2184 case 0x004d5000: /* CMP\0 */
2185 performance_msg = 1;
2186 short_length = 0;
2187 break;
2188 case 0x004c4d00: /* \0LMC reversed byte order */
2189 byte_swap = 1;
2190 case 0x004d4c00: /* CML\0 */
2191 event_msg = 1;
2192 get_attrs = 1;
2193 break;
2194 case 0x00484d00: /* \0HMC reversed byte order - handshake */
2195 byte_swap = 1;
2196 case 0x004d4800: /* CMH\0 - handshake */
2197 handshake = 1;
2198 get_attrs = 0;
2199 break;
2200 default:
2201 /* non CM message */
2202 /* lookup registered message prefixes and try to find handler */
2203 /* otherwise give up */

2205 int ret;
2206 CMbuffer local = NULL((void*)0);
2207 #ifdef EVER_HAVE_HANDLERS_OTHER_THAN_PBIO
2208 if (cm_buffer == NULL((void*)0)) {
2209 local = fill_cmbuffer(cm, buffer, length);
2210 buffer = local->buffer;
2211 }
2212 #endif

, 2213);
2214 ret = CMdo_non_CM_handler(conn, *(int*)buffer, buffer, length);
2215 CManager_lock(cm)IntCManager_lock(cm, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c"
, 2215);
2216 if (local) cm_return_data_buf(cm, local);
2217 if (ret == -1) {
2218 printf("Unknown message on connection %lx, failed %d, closed %d, %x\n", (long) conn, conn->failed, conn->closed, *(int*)buffer);
2219 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMFreeVerbose, "Calling connection unknown message failed with dereference %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMFreeVerbose) : CMtrace_val

, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) ,
CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(conn->cm

tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Calling connection unknown message failed with dereference %p\n"

2221 }
2222 return 0;
2223 }
2224 }
2225
2226 if (get_attrs == 1) {
2227 if (!event_msg) {
2228 header_len = 16;/* magic plus two 4-byte sizes (attrs + data) */
2229 skip = 4;
2230 } else {
2231 header_len = 16;
2232 }
2233 } else {
2234 if (short_length) {
2235 header_len = 8; /* magic plus 4-byte size */
2236 } else {
2237 header_len = 12; /* magic plus 8-byte size */
2238 }
2239 }
2240
2241 if (length < header_len) {
2242 return header_len - length;
2243 }
2244 base = buffer + 4 + skip; /* skip used data */
2245 if (short_length) {
2246 if (byte_swap) {
2247 int tmp;
2248 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
2249 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[0];
2250 #else
2251 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[3];
2252 #endif
2253 ((char*)&tmp)[0] = base[3];
2254 ((char*)&tmp)[1] = base[2];
2255 ((char*)&tmp)[2] = base[1];
2256 ((char*)&tmp)[3] = base[0];
2257 data_length = tmp;
2258 if (header_len != 8) {
2259 ((char*)&attr_length)[0] = base[7];
2260 ((char*)&attr_length)[1] = base[6];
2261 ((char*)&attr_length)[2] = base[5];
2262 ((char*)&attr_length)[3] = base[4];
2263 }
2264 } else {
2265 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
2266 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[3];
2267 #else
2268 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[0];
2269 #endif
2270 data_length = ((int *) base)[0];
2271 if (header_len != 8) {
2272 attr_length = ((int *) base)[1];
2273 }
2274 }
2275 } else {
2276 if (byte_swap) {
2277 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
2278 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[0];
2279 #else
2280 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[3];
2281 #endif
2282 int tmp;
2283 ((char*)&tmp)[0] = base[3];
2284 ((char*)&tmp)[1] = base[2];
2285 ((char*)&tmp)[2] = base[1];
2286 ((char*)&tmp)[3] = base[0];
2287 data_length = ((int64_t)tmp) << 32;
2288 ((char*)&tmp)[0] = base[7];
2289 ((char*)&tmp)[1] = base[6];
2290 ((char*)&tmp)[2] = base[5];
2291 ((char*)&tmp)[3] = base[4];
2292 if (header_len != 12) {
2293 ((char*)&attr_length)[0] = base[11];
2294 ((char*)&attr_length)[1] = base[10];
2295 ((char*)&attr_length)[2] = base[9];
2296 ((char*)&attr_length)[3] = base[8];
2297 }
2298 } else {
2299 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
2300 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[3];
2301 #else
2302 checksum = (unsigned char) check_sum_base[0];
2303 #endif
2304 data_length = ((int64_t)(((int *) base)[0])) << 32;
2305 data_length += ((int *) base)[1];
2306 if (header_len != 12) {
2307 attr_length = ((int *) base)[1];

2324 ((char*)&stone_id)[1] = base[10];

2326 ((char*)&stone_id)[3] = base[8];
2327 } else {

2330 }
2331

2333 return header_len + data_length + attr_length -

2340 return 0;
2341 }
2342 if (checksum != 0) {
2343 unsigned char calculated_checksum = 0;
2344 for (i=4; i < length; i++) {
2345 calculated_checksum += ((unsigned char *)buffer)[i];

2356 }
2357 }

2359 CMdo_performance_response(conn, data_length, performance_func, byte_swap,
2360 base);
2361 return 0;
2362 } else if (evcontrol_msg) {

2568
2569 void
2570 INT_CMregister_handler(CMFormat format, CMHandlerFunc handler,
2571 void *client_data)
2572 {
2573 CManager cm = format->cm;
2574 int i;
2575 format->handler = handler;
2576 format->client_data = client_data;
2577
2578 for (i=0; i< cm->in_format_count; i++) {
2579 if (cm->in_formats[i].format == format->ffsformat) {
2580 if (!cm->in_formats[i].handler) {
2581 cm->in_formats[i].handler = handler;
2582 cm->in_formats[i].client_data = client_data;
2583 } else if ((cm->in_formats[i].handler != handler) ||
2584 (cm->in_formats[i].client_data != client_data)) {
2585 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Warning, CMregister_handler() called multiple times for the same format with different handler or client_data\n");
2586 fprintf(stderrstderr, "Repeated calls will be ignored\n");
2587 }
2588 }
2589 }
2590 }

2647 int vec_count = 0;
2648 int length = 0;
2649 FFSEncodeVector vec = conn->queued_data.vector_data;
2650 int actual = 0;

2657 conn->transport_data,

2659 attrs);

2661 goto failed;
2662 }

()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Continued partial pending write, %d bytes sent\n"
, actual) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2666 while (actual > vec[i].iov_len) {
2667 actual -= vec[i].iov_len;
2668 i++;
2669 vec_count--;
2670 }
2671 vec[i].iov_len -= actual;
2672 vec[i].iov_base = (char*)vec[i].iov_base + actual;
2673 conn->queued_data.vector_data = &vec[i];

, (long)conn, vec_count) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file
);}
2675 (long)conn, vec_count){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void

);};

2677 }
2678 }
2679 if (conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free) {
2680 cm_return_data_buf(conn->cm, conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free);
2681 }
2682 conn->write_pending = 0;
2683 conn->trans->set_write_notify(conn->trans, &CMstatic_trans_svcs,
2684 conn->transport_data, 0);
2685

2688 }
2689 cm_wake_any_pending_write(conn);
2690 return;
2691 failed:
2692 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMFreeVerbose, "Calling write failed connection failed with dereference %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void

[CMFreeVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file
, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) ,
CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(conn->cm
->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.
tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Calling write failed connection failed with dereference %p\n"
, conn) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2693 INT_CMConnection_failed(conn);
2694 if (conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free) {
2695 cm_return_data_buf(conn->cm, conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free);
2696 conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free = NULL((void*)0);
2697 }
2698 conn->write_pending = 0;
2699 conn->trans->set_write_notify(conn->trans, &CMstatic_trans_svcs,
2700 conn->transport_data, 0);
2701 cm_wake_any_pending_write(conn);

2742
2743 static void
2744 queue_remaining_write(CMConnection conn, FFSEncodeVector tmp_vec,
2745 FFSEncodeVector pbio_vec, int vec_count,
2746 attr_list attrs, int actual_bytes_written,
2747 int attrs_present)
2748 {
2749 int i = 0, j = 0;
2750 int total_bytes = 0;
2751 int remaining_bytes = 0;
2752
2753 for (i=0; i < vec_count; i++) {
2754 total_bytes += tmp_vec[i].iov_len;
2755 }
2756 remaining_bytes = total_bytes - actual_bytes_written;
2757 i = 0;
2758 while (actual_bytes_written > tmp_vec[i].iov_len) {
2759 actual_bytes_written -= tmp_vec[i].iov_len;
2760 i++;
2761 }
2762 tmp_vec[i].iov_len -= actual_bytes_written;
2763 tmp_vec[i].iov_base = (char*)tmp_vec[i].iov_base + actual_bytes_written;
2764 if (pbio_vec) {
2765 if (attrs_present) {
2766 pbio_vec[i-2] = tmp_vec[i];
2767 } else {
2768 pbio_vec[i-1] = tmp_vec[i];
2769 }
2770 }
2771 actual_bytes_written = 0;
2772 /*
2773 * Data is either:
2774 * vec 0 = header
2775 * vec 1 = ffs
2776 * vec 2 = ffs
2777
2778 * vec 0 = header
2779 * vec 1 = attrs
2780 * vec 2 = ffs
2781 * vec 2 = ffs
2782
2783 * vec 0 = header
2784 * vec 1 = notffs
2785 * vec 2 = notffs
2786
2787 * vec 0 = header
2788 * vec 1 = attrs
2789 * vec 2 = notffs
2790 * vec 2 = notffs
2791 */
2792
2793 conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free = NULL((void*)0);
2794
2795 if (i == 0) {
2796 /* didn't even write the 8 or 12 or 16 or 24 byte header */
2797 assert(sizeof(conn->queued_data.rem_header) >= tmp_vec[0].iov_len)((void) sizeof ((sizeof(conn->queued_data.rem_header) >=
tmp_vec[0].iov_len) ? 1 : 0), __extension__ ({ if (sizeof(conn
->queued_data.rem_header) >= tmp_vec[0].iov_len) ; else
__assert_fail ("sizeof(conn->queued_data.rem_header) >= tmp_vec[0].iov_len"
, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c", 2797, __extension__
__PRETTY_FUNCTION__); }));
2798 memcpy(&conn->queued_data.rem_header, tmp_vec[0].iov_base,
2799 tmp_vec[0].iov_len);
2800 conn->queued_data.rem_header_len = tmp_vec[0].iov_len;
2801 } else {
2802 conn->queued_data.rem_header_len = 0;
2803 }
2804 if (attrs_present && (i <= 1)) {
2805 /* got stuck in encoded attributes */
2806 conn->queued_data.rem_attr_base = tmp_vec[1].iov_base;
2807 conn->queued_data.rem_attr_len = tmp_vec[1].iov_len;
2808 i++;
2809 } else {
2810 conn->queued_data.rem_attr_len = 0;
2811 }
2812
2813
2814 /* fixup pbio_vec */
2815 j = i - 1; /* how far into the pbio vector are we? */
2816 if (attrs_present) j--;
2817 if (j == -1) {
2818 /* no PBIO data */
2819 conn->queued_data.vector_data = NULL((void*)0);
2820 return;
2821 }
2822 if (pbio_vec == NULL((void*)0)) {
2823 /* DATA NOT FFS, don't do optimized copying */
2824 /* Errr, something smarter here */
2825 int data_length = remaining_bytes - conn->queued_data.rem_attr_len - conn->queued_data.rem_header_len;
2826 int length = data_length + (sizeof(tmp_vec[0])*2);
2827 char *ptr;
2828 CMbuffer buf = cm_get_data_buf(conn->cm, length);
2829 FFSEncodeVector vec = buf->buffer;
2830 vec[0].iov_len = data_length;
2831 vec[0].iov_base = buf->buffer + (sizeof(tmp_vec[0])*2);
2832 vec[1].iov_len = 0;
2833 vec[1].iov_base = NULL((void*)0);
2834 conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free = buf;
2835 conn->queued_data.vector_data = vec;
2836 if (i == 0) i=1;
2837 if (attrs_present && i <= 1) i=2;
2838 ptr = vec[0].iov_base;
2839 while (i < vec_count) {
2840 memcpy(ptr, tmp_vec[i].iov_base, tmp_vec[i].iov_len);
2841 ptr += tmp_vec[i].iov_len;
2842 data_length -= tmp_vec[i].iov_len;
2843 i++;
2844 }
2845 return;
2846 } else {
2847 conn->queued_data.buffer_to_free = NULL((void*)0);
2848 }
2849 if (j >= 0) {
2850 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "Removing from pbio_vec at offset %d\n", (int) j){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Removing from pbio_vec at offset %d\n"
, (int) j) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2851 pbio_vec[j].iov_len -= actual_bytes_written;
2852 pbio_vec[j].iov_base = (char*)pbio_vec[j].iov_base +
2853 actual_bytes_written;
2854 } else {
2855 j = 0; /* nothing written */
2856 }
2857
2858 /*
2859 * copy application data (which had been left in place) into temporary
2860 * PBIO buffer as well.
2861 */
2862 conn->queued_data.vector_data =
2863 copy_all_to_FFSBuffer(conn->io_out_buffer, &pbio_vec[j]);
2864 tmp_vec = conn->queued_data.vector_data;
2865 i = 0;
2866 }

2868 static void
2869 remove_pending_write_callback_by_id(CMConnection conn, int id) {
2870 assert(id < conn->write_callback_len && id >= 0)((void) sizeof ((id < conn->write_callback_len &&
id >= 0) ? 1 : 0), __extension__ ({ if (id < conn->
write_callback_len && id >= 0) ; else __assert_fail
("id < conn->write_callback_len && id >= 0"
, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c", 2870, __extension__
__PRETTY_FUNCTION__); }));
2871 conn->write_callbacks[id].func = NULL((void*)0);

2873
2874 static void
2875 remove_pending_write_callback(CMConnection conn, CMWriteCallbackFunc handler,
2876 void *client_data)
2877 {
2878 int i = 0;
2879 while (conn->write_callbacks[i].func != handler
2880 && conn->write_callbacks[i].client_data != client_data) i++;
2881 conn->write_callbacks[i].func = NULL((void*)0);
2882 }
2883
2884 static int
2885 add_pending_write_callback(CMConnection conn, CMWriteCallbackFunc handler,
2886 void* client_data)
2887 {
2888 int count = 0;
2889 while (conn->write_callbacks && count < conn->write_callback_len &&
2890 (conn->write_callbacks[count].func != NULL((void*)0))) count++;
2891 if (count + 1 > conn->write_callback_len) {
2892 if (conn->write_callbacks == NULL((void*)0)) {
2893 conn->write_callbacks = malloc(sizeof(conn->write_callbacks[0]));
2894 conn->write_callback_len = 1;
2895 } else {
2896 conn->write_callbacks =
2897 realloc(conn->write_callbacks,
2898 sizeof(conn->write_callbacks[0])*(count+1));
2899 conn->write_callback_len = count+1;
2900 }
2901 }
2902 conn->write_callbacks[count].func = handler;
2903 conn->write_callbacks[count].client_data = client_data;
2904 return count;
2905 }

2908 static void
2909 wake_pending_write(CManager cm, CMConnection conn, void *param)
2910 {
2911 int cond = (long)param;
2912 remove_pending_write_callback(conn, wake_pending_write, param);
2913 INT_CMCondition_signal(cm, cond);
2914 }

2916 void
2917 wait_for_pending_write(CMConnection conn)
2918 {
2919 CMControlList cl = conn->cm->control_list;
2920 assert(CManager_locked(conn->cm))((void) sizeof ((CManager_locked(conn->cm)) ? 1 : 0), __extension__
({ if (CManager_locked(conn->cm)) ; else __assert_fail ("CManager_locked(conn->cm)"
, "/home/chuck/Code/sst/EVPath/source/cm.c", 2920, __extension__
__PRETTY_FUNCTION__); }));
2921 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "Wait for pending write for conn %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Wait for pending write for conn %p\n"
, conn) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2922
2923 if ((!cl->has_thread) || (thr_thread_self()pthread_self() == cl->server_thread)) {
2924 /* single thread working, just poll network */
2925 while(conn->write_pending && !conn->closed) {
2926 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "Control list wait for conn %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Control list wait for conn %p\n"
, conn) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2927 CMcontrol_list_wait(cl);
2928 }
2929 } else {
2930 /* other thread is handling the network wait for it to wake us up */
2931 while (conn->write_pending && !conn->closed) {
2932 int cond = INT_CMCondition_get(conn->cm, conn);
2933 add_pending_write_callback(conn, wake_pending_write,
2934 (void*) (long)cond);
2935 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "Condition wait for conn %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Condition wait for conn %p\n"
, conn) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2936 if (INT_CMCondition_wait(conn->cm, cond) == 0) {
2937 /* condition wait failed, connection is dead */
2938 conn->write_pending = 0;
2939 }
2940 }
2941 }
2942 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose, "Done waiting for pending write for conn %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void
*)0)) ? CMtrace_init(conn->cm, CMLowLevelVerbose) : CMtrace_val
[CMLowLevelVerbose]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(conn->cm->
CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - ", (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self
()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(
conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - ", (long long)ts.
tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(conn->cm->CMTrace_file, "Done waiting for pending write for conn %p\n"
, conn) : 0);fflush(conn->cm->CMTrace_file);};
2943 }

2948 wait_for_pending_write(conn);

2958
2959 /* Returns 1 if successful, -1 if deferred, 0 on error */
2960 int
2961 INT_CMwrite_raw_notify(CMConnection conn, FFSEncodeVector full_vec, FFSEncodeVector data_vec,
2962 long vec_count, long byte_count, attr_list attrs, int data_vec_stack,
2963 CMcompletion_notify_func notify_func, void *notify_client_data)
2964 {
2965 int actual = 0;
2966 unsigned char checksum = 0;
2967 int i, j, start;
2968 long count = 0;
2969 long length = 0;
2970 if (conn->closed || conn->failed) return 0;
2971
2972 if (conn->write_pending) {
2973 wait_for_pending_write(conn);
2974 }
2975 for (i=0; i < vec_count; i++) {
2976 length += full_vec[i].iov_len;
2977 }
2978 start = 4;
2979 if (length < 10240) {
2980 /* do checksum for small messages */
2981 for (i=0; i < vec_count; i++) {
2982 count += full_vec[i].iov_len - start;
2983 for (j=start; j< full_vec[i].iov_len; j++) {
2984 checksum += ((unsigned char*)full_vec[i].iov_base)[j];
2985 }
2986 start = 0;
2987 }
2988 }
2989 ((int*)full_vec[0].iov_base)[0] =
2990 (((int*)full_vec[0].iov_base)[0] & 0xffffff00) | (unsigned char) checksum;
2991 if ((conn->do_non_blocking_write == 1) && (conn->trans->NBwritev_func)) {
2992 int actual_bytes;
2993 actual_bytes =
2994 conn->trans->NBwritev_func(&CMstatic_trans_svcs,
2995 conn->transport_data,
2996 full_vec, vec_count, attrs);
2997 if (actual_bytes < 0) {
2998 CMtrace_out(conn->cm, CMFreeVerbose, "Calling write failed connection failed with dereference %p\n", conn){struct timespec ts ; (((conn->cm->CMTrace_file == ((void

3364
3365 static void
3366 init_non_blocking_conn(CMConnection conn)
3367 {
3368 /* default */
3369 conn->do_non_blocking_write = 0;
3370
3371 if (conn->trans->NBwritev_func == NULL((void*)0)) return;
3372 if (conn->trans->set_write_notify == NULL((void*)0)) return;
3373
3374 /* only if we make it this far should we try non blocking writes */
3375 conn->do_non_blocking_write = 1;
3376 }
3377
3378 extern int
3379 INT_CMConnection_write_would_block(CMConnection conn)
3380 {
3381 if (conn->do_non_blocking_write == -1) {
3382 init_non_blocking_conn(conn);
3383 }
3384 return conn->write_pending;
3385 }
3386
3387 extern int
3388 INT_CMregister_write_callback(CMConnection conn, CMWriteCallbackFunc handler,
3389 void *client_data)
3390 {
3391 if (conn->do_non_blocking_write == -1) {
3392 init_non_blocking_conn(conn);
3393 }
3394 return add_pending_write_callback(conn, handler, client_data);
3395 }
3396
3397 extern void
3398 INT_CMunregister_write_callback(CMConnection conn, int id)
3399 {
3400 remove_pending_write_callback_by_id(conn, id);
3401 }

3441 extern CMTaskHandle
3442 INT_CMadd_periodic(CManager cm, long period, CMPollFunc func,
3443 void *client_data)
3444 {
3445 CMTaskHandle handle = INT_CMmalloc(sizeof(*handle));
3446 if (!cm->control_list->select_initialized) {
3447 CM_init_select(cm->control_list, cm);
3448 }
3449 handle->cm = cm;
3450 handle->task =
3451 cm->control_list->add_periodic(&CMstatic_trans_svcs,
3452 &cm->control_list->select_data,
3453 0, period, (select_list_func)func,
3454 (void*)cm, client_data);
3455 if (handle->task == NULL((void*)0)) {
3456 free(handle);
3457 return NULL((void*)0);
3458 }
3459 return handle;
3460 }

3651 typedef struct foreign_handler_struct {
3652 int header;
3653 CMNonCMHandler handler;
3654 } *handler_list;
3655
3656 static handler_list foreign_handler_list;
3657 static int foreign_handler_count = 0;
3658
3659 extern void
3660 INT_CMregister_non_CM_message_handler(int header, CMNonCMHandler handler)
3661 {
3662 if (foreign_handler_count > 0) {
3663 foreign_handler_list = INT_CMrealloc(foreign_handler_list,
3664 sizeof(foreign_handler_list[0]) *
3665 (foreign_handler_count + 1));
3666 } else {
3667 foreign_handler_list = INT_CMmalloc(sizeof(foreign_handler_list[0]));
3668 }
3669 foreign_handler_list[foreign_handler_count].header = header;
3670 foreign_handler_list[foreign_handler_count].handler = handler;
3671 foreign_handler_count++;
3672 }
3673
3674 int
3675 CMdo_non_CM_handler(CMConnection conn, int header, char *buffer, int length)
3676 {
3677 int i = 0;
3678 while (i < foreign_handler_count) {
3679 if (foreign_handler_list[i].header == header) {
3680 return foreign_handler_list[i].handler(conn, conn->trans, buffer,
3681 length);
3682 }
3683 i++;
3684 }
3685 return -1;
3686 }

3700static
3701int offset_compare(const void* lhsv, const void* rhsv)
3702 {
3703 CMavail_period_ptr lhs = (CMavail_period_ptr) lhsv;
3704 CMavail_period_ptr rhs = (CMavail_period_ptr) rhsv;
3705 if (lhs->offset.tv_sec < rhs->offset.tv_sec)
3706 return -1;
3707 if (lhs->offset.tv_sec > rhs->offset.tv_sec)
3708 return 1;
3709 return lhs->offset.tv_usec - rhs->offset.tv_usec;
3710 }
3711
3712extern int
3713INT_CMinstall_pull_schedule(CManager cm, struct timeval *base_time,
3714 struct timeval *period, CMavail_period_ptr avail)
3715{
3716 int i = 0, count = 0;
3717 struct timeval zero = {0,0}, last_end = {0,0};
3718 CMavail_period_ptr sorted;
3719 while (timercmp(&avail[count].offset, &zero, !=)(((&avail[count].offset)->tv_sec == (&zero)->tv_sec
) ? ((&avail[count].offset)->tv_usec != (&zero)->
tv_usec) : ((&avail[count].offset)->tv_sec != (&zero
)->tv_sec)) ||
3720 timercmp(&avail[count].duration, &zero, !=)(((&avail[count].duration)->tv_sec == (&zero)->
tv_sec) ? ((&avail[count].duration)->tv_usec != (&
zero)->tv_usec) : ((&avail[count].duration)->tv_sec
!= (&zero)->tv_sec))) {
3721 if (avail[count].offset.tv_sec < 0) {
3722 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail sec offset is negative. Rejected\n");
3723 return 0;
3724 }
3725 if (avail[count].offset.tv_usec < 0) {
3726 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail usec offset is negative. Rejected\n");
3727 return 0;
3728 }
3729 if (avail[count].duration.tv_sec < 0) {
3730 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail sec duration is negative. Rejected\n");
3731 return 0;
3732 }
3733 if (avail[count].duration.tv_usec < 0) {
3734 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail usec duration is negative. Rejected\n");
3735 return 0;
3736 }
3737 count++;
3738 }
3739 sorted = malloc(sizeof(avail[0]) * (count+1));
3740 memcpy(sorted, avail, sizeof(avail[0]) * count);
3741 qsort(sorted, count, sizeof(avail[0]), offset_compare);
3742 for (i = 0; i < count; i++) {
3743 struct timeval end;
3744 timeradd(&avail[i].offset, &avail[i].duration, &end)do { (&end)->tv_sec = (&avail[i].offset)->tv_sec
+ (&avail[i].duration)->tv_sec; (&end)->tv_usec
= (&avail[i].offset)->tv_usec + (&avail[i].duration
)->tv_usec; if ((&end)->tv_usec >= 1000000) { ++
(&end)->tv_sec; (&end)->tv_usec -= 1000000; } }
while (0);
3745 if (timercmp(&end, period, >)(((&end)->tv_sec == (period)->tv_sec) ? ((&end)
->tv_usec > (period)->tv_usec) : ((&end)->tv_sec
> (period)->tv_sec))) {
3746 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail region %d rejected, extends beyond period\n", i);
3747 free(sorted);
3748 return -1;
3749 }
3750 if (timercmp(&avail[i].offset, &last_end, <)(((&avail[i].offset)->tv_sec == (&last_end)->tv_sec
) ? ((&avail[i].offset)->tv_usec < (&last_end)->
tv_usec) : ((&avail[i].offset)->tv_sec < (&last_end
)->tv_sec))) {
3751 fprintf(stderrstderr, "CMinstall_pull_schedule(), avail regions overlap. Rejected\n");
3752 free(sorted);
3753 return -1;
3754 }
3755 last_end = end;
3756 }
3757
3758 cm->base_time = *base_time;
3759 cm->period = *period;
3760 cm->avail = sorted;
3761 transport_entry *trans_list;
3762 trans_list = cm->transports;
3763 CMtrace_out(cm, CMTransportVerbose, "CM installed pull schedule with period %ld secs, %ld usecs\n", period->tv_sec, (long) period->tv_usec){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?
CMtrace_init(cm, CMTransportVerbose) : CMtrace_val[CMTransportVerbose
]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - "
, (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing
? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file
, "CM installed pull schedule with period %ld secs, %ld usecs\n"
, period->tv_sec, (long) period->tv_usec) : 0);fflush(cm
->CMTrace_file);};
3764 while ((trans_list != NULL((void*)0)) && (*trans_list != NULL((void*)0))) {
3765 if ((*trans_list)->install_pull_schedule_func) {
3766 (*trans_list)->install_pull_schedule_func(&CMstatic_trans_svcs,
3767 *trans_list,
3768 base_time, period,
3769 cm->avail);
3770 CMtrace_out(cm, CMTransportVerbose, "CM installed pull schedule to transport %s\n", (*trans_list)->trans_name){struct timespec ts ; (((cm->CMTrace_file == ((void*)0)) ?
CMtrace_init(cm, CMTransportVerbose) : CMtrace_val[CMTransportVerbose
]) ? (CMtrace_PID ? fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "P%lxT%lx - "
, (long) getpid(), (long)pthread_self()) : 0) , CMtrace_timing
? clock_gettime(1, &ts),fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file, "%lld.%.9ld - "
, (long long)ts.tv_sec, ts.tv_nsec):0, fprintf(cm->CMTrace_file
, "CM installed pull schedule to transport %s\n", (*trans_list
)->trans_name) : 0);fflush(cm->CMTrace_file);};
3771 }
3772 trans_list++;
3773 }
3774 return 0;
